Function EncryptPassword(strPassword)
  strPassword=ucase(trim(strPassword))
  for i = 1 to len(strPassword)
     EncryptPassword = EncryptPassword & chr(asc(mid(strPassword,i,1))+100)
  next
End Function

Function DecryptPassword(strPassword)
  strPassword=ucase(trim(strPassword))
  for i = 1 to len(strPassword)
     DecryptPassword = DecryptPassword & chr(asc(mid(strPassword,i,1))-100)
  next
End Function

'06202024: SPagara: Additional for Roundup
Function RoundUp(n)
n = Int(n*1000+0.999999)/1000
RoundUp = formatnumber(n, 2)
End Function

'Excise Tax
if UCase(strStatus) = "C" AND (CInt(mid(ApplNumber,6,2)) > 4 OR Year(NOW) > 2019)  then
set rsCons = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
rsCons.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
rsCons.Source = "SELECT IsNull(ExciseType, '') as ExciseType, IsNull(ExciseRate, '') as ExciseRate, IsNull(ExciseQty, '') as ExciseQty, IsNull(ExciseUnit, '') as ExciseUnit, IsNull(ExciseTotal, '') as ExciseTotal, InvValue, OCharges, HSCode, SupVal1, IsNull(TarSpec, '') as TarSpec, ItemNo, HSCode_TAR, Pref, MSP, Id FROM dbo.TBLIMPAPL_CONS WHERE ApplNo = '" & ApplNumber & "' ORDER BY ItemNo"
rsCons.CursorType = 1
rsCons.CursorLocation = 3
rsCons.LockType = 3
rsCons.Open()
rsCons_numRows = 0

	if NOT rsCons.EOF then
	
			'get total Invoice Value
			set rsConsTot = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
			rsConsTot.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
			rsConsTot.Source = "Select Sum(InvValue) as TOTALVALUE from TBLIMPAPL_CONS where APPLNO='" & ApplNumber & "'"
			rsConsTot.CursorType = 1
			rsConsTot.CursorLocation = 3
			rsConsTot.LockType = 3
			rsConsTot.Open()
			rsConsTot_numRows = 0
			
			TOTALVALUE = rsConsTot("TOTALVALUE")
			rsConsTot.Close()
		
			while NOT rsCons.EOF
				set rsFIN = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
				rsFIN.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
				rsFIN.Source = "SELECT WOBankCharge, isnull(EXCHRATE, 0) as EXCHRATE, CustCurr, FreightCost, FreightCurr, InsCost, InsCurr, OtherCost, OtherCurr, ArrasCost, WharCost FROM dbo.TBLIMPAPL_FIN WHERE ApplNo = '" & ApplNumber & "'"
				rsFIN.CursorType = 1
				rsFIN.CursorLocation = 3
				rsFIN.LockType = 3
				rsFIN.Open()
				rsFIN_numRows = 0

				If NOT rsFIN.EOF then
					'get Freight Value per item
					ITEMVALUE = cDbl(rsCons("InvValue"))
					IFREIGHT = 0
					if (rsFIN("exchrate") <> "" OR rsFIN("exchrate") <> 0) then
						strRate = rsFIN("EXCHRATE")
					else
						set rseR8 = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
						rseR8.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
						rseR8.Source = "SELECT TOP 1 RAT_EXC FROM GBRATTAB WHERE (CUR_COD = 'USD') ORDER BY EEA_DOV DESC"
						rseR8.CursorType = 1
						rseR8.CursorLocation = 3
						rseR8.LockType = 3
						rseR8.Open()
						rseR8_numrows =0
						
						strRate = rseR8("RAT_EXC")
						rseR8.Close()
					end if
						
																																	
					strFCurr = rsFIN("FreightCurr")
					
					if Trim("" & rsFIN("FreightCost")) = "" then
						intFCost = 0
					Else
						intFCost = cDbl(rsFIN("FreightCost"))
					End If
					
					If intFCost <> 0 Then
					   If strFCurr <> "PHP" Then
						  '06202024: SPagara: Update on Computation
					        IFREIGHT = RoundUp(Round(cDbl(ITEMVALUE) / cDbl(TOTALVALUE) * (cDbl(intFCost)),2) * cDbl(strRate))
                         'IFREIGHT = (cDbl(intFCost) * cDbl(strRate)) * (cDbl(ITEMVALUE) / cDbl(TOTALVALUE))
					   Else
						 IFREIGHT = cDbl(intFCost) * (cDbl(ITEMVALUE) / cDbl(TOTALVALUE))
					   End If
					End If
					
					'get Insurance Value per item
					IINS = 0
					strICurr = rsFIN("InsCurr")
					strInsCost	= rsFIN("InsCost")
					
					If trim(strInsCost) = "" or IsNull(strInsCost) = True then
						strInsCost = 0
					Else
						strInsCost = cDbl(strInsCost)
					End If
					
					If strICurr <> "PHP" Then
					   '06202024: SPagara: Update on Computation
				        C1 = RoundUp(Round(cDbl(ITEMVALUE) / cDbl(TOTALVALUE) * (cDbl(strInsCost)),2) * cDbl(strRate))
                       'C1 = cDbl(strInsCost) * cDbl(strRate) * (cDbl(ITEMVALUE) / cDbl(TOTALVALUE))
					Else
					   C1 = cDbl(strInsCost) * (cDbl(ITEMVALUE) / cDbl(TOTALVALUE))
					End If
					
					If strICurr <> "PHP" Then
					   C2 = cDbl(ITEMVALUE) * cDbl(strRate) * 0
					Else
					   C2 = cDbl(ITEMVALUE) * 0
					End If
					
					If C1 > C2 then
						'06192024: SPagara: Update on Computation
				        IINS = RoundUp(cDbl(C1))
                        'IINS = cDbl(C1)
					Else
						'06192024: SPagara: Update on Computation
					    IINS = RoundUp(cDbl(C2))
                        'IINS = cDbl(C2)
					end if
					
					'get Other Cost Value per item
					OCOST = 0
					strOCurr = rsFIN("OtherCurr")
					strOCost = rsFIN("OtherCost")
					
					If rsCons("OCharges") =  True Then
						OCOST = 0
					Else
						If trim(strOCost) = "" or IsNull(strOCost) = True then
							strOCost = 0
						Else
							strOCost = cDbl(strOCost)
						End If
						If strOCost = 0 Then
							If strOCurr <> "PHP" Then
							   OCOST = cDbl(ITEMVALUE) * cDbl(strRate) * 0.03
							Else
							   OCOST = cDbl(ITEMVALUE) * 0.03
							End If
						Else
							If strOCurr <> "PHP" Then
							   '06202024: SPagara: Update on Computation
						        OCOST =  RoundUp(Round(cDbl(ITEMVALUE) / cDbl(TOTALVALUE) * (cDbl(strOCost)),2) * cDbl(strRate))
                               'OCOST = cDbl(strOCost) * cDbl(strRate) * (cDbl(ITEMVALUE) / cDbl(TOTALVALUE))
							Else
							   OCOST = cDbl(strOCost) * (cDbl(ITEMVALUE) / cDbl(TOTALVALUE))
							End If
						End If
					End If
					
					'compute for Dutiable Value per item
					strDVCurr = rsFIN("CustCurr")
					
					If strDVCurr <> "PHP" Then
                        '06202024: SPagara: Update on Computation
					    DVAL = RoundUp((cDbl(ITEMVALUE) * cDbl(strRate)) + cDbl(IFREIGHT) + cDbl(IINS) + cDbl(OCOST))
						DVAL1 = (ITEMVALUE * strRate)  + IFREIGHT + IINS + OCOST
                       'DVAL = Round((cDbl(ITEMVALUE) * cDbl(strRate)),0) + Round(cDbl(IFREIGHT),0) + Round(cDbl(IINS),0) + Round(cDbl(OCOST),0)
					Else
					   DVAL = Round(cDbl(ITEMVALUE),0) + Round(cDbl(IFREIGHT),0) + Round(cDbl(IINS),0) + Round(cDbl(OCOST),0)
					   DVAL1 = (ITEMVALUE * strRate)  + IFREIGHT + IINS + OCOST
					End If
					
					Dim strHSCode1
					Dim strHSCode2
					Dim strTARPR2
					Dim TarRate
					Dim PrefRate
					
					strHSCode1 = Mid((rsCons("HSCode")), 1, 6)
					strHSCode2 = Mid((rsCons("HSCode")), 7, 2)
					strTARPR2 = rsCons("HSCODE_TAR")
					PrefRate = rsCons("Pref")
					
					set rsTar = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
					rsTar.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
					rsTar.Source = "Select *, Isnull(Tar_t01,'') as Tar_t01, Isnull(Tar_t02,'') as Tar_t02, Isnull(Tar_t03,'') as Tar_t03, Isnull(Tar_t05,'') as Tar_t05, Isnull(Tar_t06,'') as Tar_t06, Isnull(Tar_t07,'') as Tar_t07, Isnull(Tar_t08,'') as Tar_t08, Isnull(Tar_t09,'') as Tar_t09, Isnull(Tar_t10,'') as Tar_t10, Isnull(Tar_t11,'') as Tar_t11, Isnull(Tar_t12,'') as Tar_t12, Isnull(Tar_t13,'') as Tar_t13, Isnull(Tar_t14,'') as Tar_t14 from GBTARTAB where Hs6_cod='" & strHSCode1 & "' and tar_pr1='" & strHSCode2 & "' and tar_pr2='" & strTARPR2 & "'"
					rsTar.CursorType = 1
					rsTar.CursorLocation = 3
					rsTar.LockType = 3
					rsTar.Open()
					rsTar_numRows = 0
					
					if NOT rsTar.EOF then
						if PrefRate = "" or PrefRate = "None" or Prefrate = "NONE" then
			                if NOT rsTar.EOF then
				                if rsTar("Tar_t01") <> "" and NOT IsNull(rsTar("Tar_t01")) then
					                TarRate = cDbl(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t01").Value)
				                else
					                TarRate = ""
				                end if
			                else
				                TarRate = ""
			                end if
			                'Response.Write(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t01").Value)
		                end if
		                if Prefrate = "AFTA" OR Prefrate = "ATIGA" then	
			                if NOT rsTar.EOF then
				                if rsTar("Tar_t02") <> "" and NOT IsNull(rsTar("Tar_t02")) then
					                TarRate = cDbl(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t02").Value)
				                else
					                TarRate = ""
				                end if
			                else
				                TarRate = ""
			                end if
			                'Response.Write(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t02").Value)
		                end if
		                if Prefrate = "AKFTA" then	
			                if NOT rsTar.EOF then
				                if rsTar("Tar_t03") <> "" and NOT IsNull(rsTar("Tar_t03")) then
					                TarRate = cDbl(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t03").Value)
				                else
					                TarRate = ""
				                end if
			                else
				                TarRate = ""
			                end if
			                'Response.Write(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t03").Value)
		                end if

		                if Prefrate = "TAR_T04" then	
			                if NOT rsTar.EOF then
				                if rsTar("Tar_t04") <> "" and NOT IsNull(rsTar("Tar_t04")) then
					                TarRate = cDbl(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t04").Value)
				                else
					                TarRate = ""
				                end if
			                else
				                TarRate = ""
			                end if
			                'Response.Write(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t03").Value)
		                end if

		                if Prefrate = "BOI" then
			                if NOT rsTar.EOF then
				                if rsTar("Tar_t05") <> "" and NOT IsNull(rsTar("Tar_t05")) then
					                TarRate = cDbl(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t05").Value)
				                else
					                TarRate = ""
				                end if
			                else
				                TarRate = ""
			                end if
			                'Response.Write(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t05").Value)
		                end if

		                if Prefrate = "JPEPA" then	
			                if NOT rsTar.EOF then
				                if rsTar("Tar_t06") <> "" and NOT IsNull(rsTar("Tar_t06")) then
					                TarRate = cDbl(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t06").Value)
				                else
					                TarRate = ""
				                end if
			                else
				                TarRate = ""
			                end if
			                'Response.Write(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t06").Value)
		                end if

		                if Prefrate = "EFTA" then	
			                if NOT rsTar.EOF then
				                if rsTar("Tar_t07") <> "" and NOT IsNull(rsTar("Tar_t07")) then
					                TarRate = cDbl(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t07").Value)
				                else
					                TarRate = ""
				                end if
			                else
				                TarRate = ""
			                end if
			                'Response.Write(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t07").Value)
		                end if

		                if Prefrate = "EFTANO" then 'Prefrate = "AICOB" or 
			                if NOT rsTar.EOF then
				                if rsTar("Tar_t09") <> "" and NOT IsNull(rsTar("Tar_t09")) then
					                TarRate = cDbl(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t09").Value)
				                else
					                TarRate = ""
				                end if	
			                else
				                TarRate = ""
			                end if
			                'Response.Write(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t09").Value)
		                end if

		                if Prefrate = "AIFTA" then	'Prefrate = "AICOC" OR 
			                if NOT rsTar.EOF then
				                if rsTar("Tar_t10") <> "" and NOT IsNull(rsTar("Tar_t10")) then
					                TarRate = cDbl(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t10").Value)
				                else
					                TarRate = ""
				                end if
			                else
				                TarRate = ""
			                end if
			                'Response.Write(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t10").Value)
		                end if

		                if Prefrate = "AJCEP" then	'Prefrate = "AISP" OR 
			                if NOT rsTar.EOF then
				                if rsTar("Tar_t11") <> "" and NOT IsNull(rsTar("Tar_t11")) then
					                TarRate = cDbl(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t11").Value)
				                else
					                TarRate = ""
				                end if
			                else
				                TarRate = ""
			                end if
			                'Response.Write(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t11").Value)
		                end if

		                if Prefrate = "EFTACL" then	'Prefrate = "AICOD" or 
			                if NOT rsTar.EOF then
				                if rsTar("Tar_t12") <> "" and NOT IsNull(rsTar("Tar_t12")) then
					                TarRate = cDbl(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t12").Value)
				                else
					                TarRate = ""
				                end if
			                else
				                TarRate = ""
			                end if
			                'Response.Write(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t12").Value)
		                end if

		                if Prefrate = "ACFTA" then	
			                if NOT rsTar.EOF then
				                if rsTar("Tar_t13") <> "" and NOT IsNull(rsTar("Tar_t13")) then
					                TarRate = cDbl(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t13").Value)
				                else
					                TarRate = ""
				                end if
			                else
				                TarRate = ""
			                end if
			                'Response.Write(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t13").Value)
		                end if

		                if Prefrate = "ANFTA" then	'Prefrate = "AICOE" OR 
			                if NOT rsTar.EOF then
				                if rsTar("Tar_t14") <> "" and NOT IsNull(rsTar("Tar_t14")) then
					                TarRate = cDbl(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t14").Value)
				                else
					                TarRate = ""
				                end if
			                else
				                TarRate = ""
			                end if
			                'Response.Write(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t14").Value)
		                end if

		                if Prefrate = "TAR_T15" then	
			                if NOT rsTar.EOF then
				                if rsTar("Tar_t15") <> "" and NOT IsNull(rsTar("Tar_t15")) then
					                TarRate = cDbl(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t15").Value)
				                else
					                TarRate = ""
				                end if
			                else
				                TarRate = ""
			                end if
			                'Response.Write(rsTar.Fields.Item("Tar_t03").Value)
		                end if
					else
						TarRate = ""
					end if 
					
					
					If TarRate <> "" then
						ITEMCUD = cDbl(DVAL) * (cDbl(cDbl(TarRate) / 100))
						TotCUD = cDbl(TotCUD + round(cDbl(ITEMCUD),0))
					else
						ITEMCUD = 0
						TotCUD = cDbl(TotCUD)
					end if
					rsTar.Close()
					
					If strFCurr <> "PHP" Then
						iFrghtTOT = intFCost * cDbl(strRate)
					else
						iFrghtTOT = intFCost
					end if
					
					If strICurr <> "PHP" Then
						iINStot = strInsCost * cDbl(strRate)
					else
						iINStot = strInsCost
					end if
					
					If strOCurr <> "PHP" Then
						iOCSTtot = strOCost * cDbl(strRate)
					else
						iOCSTtot = strOCost
					end if
					
					If strDVCurr <> "PHP" Then
					   DVALtot = Round((cDbl(TOTALVALUE) * cDbl(strRate)),0) + Round(cDbl(iFrghtTOT),0) + Round(cDbl(iINStot),0) + Round(cDbl(iOCSTtot),0)
					Else
					   DVALtot = Round(cDbl(TOTALVALUE),0) + Round(cDbl(iFrghtTOT),0) + Round(cDbl(iINStot),0) + Round(cDbl(iOCSTtot),0)
					End If
					
					Dim IBANK
					If rsCons.RecordCount > 0 then
						If rsFin.RecordCount > 0 then
							If rsFIN("WOBankCharge") = True Then
								IBANK = 0                      '---- if no bank is involved in payment
							Else
								'---- Itemized Bank Charges = (Total Dutiable Value x 0.00125) / Total Number of Items
								IBANK = (DVALtot * 0.00125) '/ TOTALITEM
							End If
							IBANK = Round(IBANK, 1)
						End If
					End If
					
					IBankperItem = (ITEMVALUE / TOTALVALUE) * IBANK
					
					set recset1 = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
					recset1.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
					recset1.Source = "Select * from dbo.ITMBRKFEE WHERE (NOT (DUTMIN IS NULL)) order by DUTMIN"
					recset1.CursorType = 1
					recset1.CursorLocation = 3
					recset1.LockType = 3
					recset1.Open()
					recset1_numRows = 0

                    '06062024: SPagara: brokerage fee
				    if (UCase(Session("mod_cod")) <> "IES") then					
					    If recset1.RecordCount > 0 then
						    '---- Get Brokerage fee
						    If cDbl(DVALtot) > 200000 Then             
						    '---- if total dutiable value is greater than 200,000.00 ||| replaced TotDuty
							    'IBROKE = ((cDbl(TotDuty) - 200000) * 0.00125) + 3543.75
							    recset1.MoveLast
							    IBROKE = ((cDbl(DVALtot) - 200000) * 0.00125) + cDbl(recset1("BrokFee"))
						    Else
							    Do While Not recset1.EOF         '---- check for item brokerage fee in the brokerage fee table
								    If cdbl(DVALtot) >= cdbl(recset1("DUTMIN")) AND cdbl(DVALtot) <= cdbl(recset1("DUTMAX")) Then
									    IBROKE = cDbl(recset1("BrokFee"))
								    End If
								    recset1.MoveNext
							    Loop
						    End If
					    End If
                    else
					    IBROKE = 700
				    end if
					recset1.Close()
					
					IBROKEperItem = IBROKE / rsCons.RecordCount
					
					'06062024: SPagara: update on doc stamp
				    if Session("mod_cod") = "IES" then
					    DocStampperItem = 130 / rsCons.RecordCount
				    else
					    DocStampperItem = 280 / rsCons.RecordCount
				    end if

					'---5/3/2000 to user dynamic value of Declaration mode IPF and Documentary stamp
					'06062024: SPagara: update for IPC
				    If Mid(Session("mod_cod"), 1, 1) = "4" OR Mid(Session("mod_cod"), 1, 1) = "7" OR Session("mod_cod") = "IES" OR Session("mod_cod") = "IE" OR Session("mod_cod") = "IED" OR Session("mod_cod") = "IEP"  Then
						set rsBroke = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
						rsBroke.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
						rsBroke.Source = "Select * from dbo.IMPPROCFEE WHERE (NOT (DUTMIN IS NULL)) order by DUTMIN"
						rsBroke.CursorType = 1
						rsBroke.CursorLocation = 3
						rsBroke.LockType = 3
						rsBroke.Open()
						rsBroke_numRows = 0
					
						Do While Not rsBroke.EOF
							If DVALtot >= rsBroke("DUTMIN") And DVALtot <= rsBroke("DUTMAX") Then
								dblIpf = rsBroke("IPF")
							End If
							rsBroke.MoveNext
						Loop
						rsBroke.Close()
					Else
						dblIpf = 250
					End If
					
					IPFperIem = dblIpf / rsCons.RecordCount
					
					'count items
					ItemCount = rsCons.RecordCount
					
					ArrasCostperIem = (ITEMVALUE / TOTALVALUE) * rsFin("ArrasCost")
					
					WharCostperIem = (ITEMVALUE / TOTALVALUE) * rsFin("WharCost")

					LandedCostPerItem = DVAL + ITEMCUD + IBankperItem + IBROKEperItem + ArrasCostperIem + WharCostperIem + DocStampperItem + IPFperIem
					
					'check Excise type
					set rsExcise = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
					rsExcise.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
					rsExcise.Source = "SELECT Type, Rate, AHTN FROM tblExcise WHERE AHTN = '"& rsCons("HSCode") &"' AND TarSpec = '" & rsCons("TARSPEC") & "'"
					rsExcise.CursorType = 0
					rsExcise.CursorLocation = 2
					rsExcise.LockType = 3
					rsExcise.Open()
					rsExcise_numRows = 0
					
					if rsExcise.EOF then
						set rsExcise1 = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
						rsExcise1.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
						rsExcise1.Source = "SELECT Type, Rate, AHTN FROM tblExcise WHERE AHTN = '"& rsCons("HSCode") &"'"
						rsExcise1.CursorType = 0
						rsExcise1.CursorLocation = 2
						rsExcise1.LockType = 3
						rsExcise1.Open()
						rsExcise1_numRows = 0
					end if
					
					'check AICODE
					set rsAiCode = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
					rsAiCode.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
					rsAiCode.Source  = "SELECT HSCODE, [Type], Rate FROM CWSAICODE WHERE HSCODE = '"& rsCons("HSCode") &"' AND HSCODE_TAR = '"& rsCons("HSCode_TAR") &"' AND TarSpec = '"& TarSpec &"' "
					rsAiCode.CursorType = 0
					rsAiCode.CursorLocation = 2
					rsAiCode.LockType = 3
					rsAiCode.Open()
					rsAiCode_numRows = 0
					
					If NOT rsAiCode.EOF THEN
						if not rsExcise.eof then
							EXTAX = rsExcise("Type")
						else
							if not rsExcise1.eof then
								EXTAX = rsExcise1("Type")
							else
								EXTAX = ""
							end if
						end if
						exciseRate = rsAiCode("Rate")
						AHTNs = rsAiCode("HSCODE")
					Else
						if NOT rsExcise.EOF then
							EXTAX = rsExcise("Type")
							exciseRate = rsExcise("Rate")
							AHTNs = rsExcise("AHTN")
						else
							if not rsExcise1.eof then
								EXTAX = rsExcise1("Type")
								exciseRate = rsExcise1("Rate")
								AHTNs = rsExcise1("AHTN")
							else
								EXTAX = ""
								exciseRate = 0
								AHTNs = ""
								strTarSpec = ""
							end if
						end if
					End If
					
					rsAiCode.Close()
					rsExcise.Close()
					
					
					if UCase(EXTAX) = "PETROLEUM" OR UCase(EXTAX) = "WINE" OR UCase(EXTAX) = "SPIRITS" OR UCase(EXTAX) = "LIQUOR" then
						ExciseTax = rsCons("SupVal1") * cdbl(exciseRate)
						EXCRate = exciseRate
						EXCQty = rsCons("SupVal1")
					elseif UCase(EXTAX) = "BEVERAGE" then
						if rsCons("TarSpec") = "1001" then
							ExciseTax = rsCons("SupVal1") * 12
							EXCRate = 12
							EXCQty = rsCons("SupVal1")
						elseif rsCons("TarSpec") = "1002" then
							ExciseTax = rsCons("SupVal1") * 6
							EXCRate = 6
							EXCQty = rsCons("SupVal1")
						elseif rsCons("TarSpec") = "1003" then
							ExciseTax = rsCons("SupVal1") * 0
							EXCRate = 0
							EXCQty = rsCons("SupVal1")
						end if
					'07102024: SPagara: Add ANd (rsCons("HSCode") <>  "25239000" AND rsCons("HSCode") <> "25232990") 
					elseif UCase(EXTAX) = "MINERALS" ANd (rsCons("HSCode") <>  "25239000" AND rsCons("HSCode") <> "25232990") then
						'07052024: Update on Minerals
						ExciseTax =  cDbl(DVAL) * 0.04
						EXCRate = 4
						EXCQty = cDbl(DVAL)
					elseif UCase(EXTAX) = "TOBACCO" then
						ExciseTax = rsCons("SupVal1") * cdbl(exciseRate)
						EXCRate = exciseRate
						EXCQty = rsCons("SupVal1")
					elseif UCase(EXTAX) = "VAPE" then
						if rsCons("TarSpec") = "1001" then
							ExciseTax = rsCons("SupVal1") * 0
							EXCRate = 0
							EXCQty = rsCons("SupVal1")
						elseif rsCons("TarSpec") = "1002" then
							' Spagara: 01092024: Update 52/ml to 54.60/ml
							ExciseTax = rsCons("SupVal1") * 54600
							EXCRate = 54.60
							EXCQty = rsCons("SupVal1")
						elseif rsCons("TarSpec") = "" then
							' Spagara: 01092024: Update 60/10ml to 64/10ml
							' Carie: 03202024: Update 64/10ml to 63/10ml
							ExciseTax = rsCons("SupVal1") * 6300
							EXCRate = 63
							EXCQty = rsCons("SupVal1")
						end if
					
					'Spagara: 07042024 additional	
					elseif UCase(EXTAX) = "PERFUME" OR (UCase(EXTAX) = "JEWELRY" and  rsCons("HSCODE") <> "90049090" and rsCons("HSCODE_tar") <> "000")  then

					ExciseTax = ((DVAL * exciseRate) / 100)
					EXCRate = exciseRate
					EXCQty = cdbl(DVAL)
					
					'Spagara: 07042024 update for jewelry
					
					elseif UCase(EXTAX) = "JEWELRY" and  rsCons("HSCODE") = "90049090" and rsCons("HSCODE_tar") = "000" then
					
						if ((UCase(Session("mod_cod")) <> "7") AND (UCase(Session("mod_cod")) <> "7T7") AND (UCase(Session("mod_cod")) <> "8ZN") AND (UCase(Session("mod_cod")) <> "8ZE") AND (UCase(Session("mod_cod")) <> "8PP") AND (UCase(Session("mod_cod")) <> "8PE")) then

							if rsCons("TarSpec") = "1001" then
								ExciseTax =  0
								EXCRate = 0
								EXCQty = rsCons("SupVal1")
							else

								ExciseTax = ((DVAL1 * 20) / 100)
								EXCRate = 20
								EXCQty = rsCons("SupVal1")
							end if
						else
							
								ExciseTax = ((DVAL1 * 20) / 100)
								EXCRate = 20
								EXCQty = rsCons("SupVal1")

						end if
					elseif UCase(EXTAX) = "PHARMACEUTICALS" then
						set chkRULCOD = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
						chkRULCOD.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
						chkRULCOD.Source = "SELECT rul_cod FROM GBTARTAB WHERE hs6_cod+tar_pr1='" & rsCons("HSCode") & "' AND tar_pr2='" & rsCons("HSCODE_TAR") & "'"
						chkRULCOD.CursorType = 0
						chkRULCOD.CursorLocation = 2
						chkRULCOD.LockType = 3
						chkRULCOD.Open()

						If NOT chkRULCOD.EOF THEN
							If chkRULCOD("rul_cod") = "EXC-300390" Then
									ExciseTax = aicodeRate * rsCons("SupVal1")
							End If
						END IF
					else
						ExciseTax = 0
						EXCRate = 0
						EXCQty = 0
					end if
					
					'get total Dutiable Value and total Excise Tax
					TOTALDVAL = CDbl(TOTALDVAL) + Round(cDbl(DVAL),2)
					TotalExciseTax = CDbl(TotalExciseTax) + cDbl(ExcTax)
					
					set rsGBTARTAB = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
					rsGBTARTAB.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
					rsGBTARTAB.Source = "SELECT rul_cod FROM GBTARTAB WHERE hs6_cod+tar_pr1='" & rsCons("HSCode") & "' AND tar_pr2='" & rsCons("HSCODE_TAR") & "'"
					rsGBTARTAB.CursorType = 0
					rsGBTARTAB.CursorLocation = 2
					rsGBTARTAB.LockType = 3
					rsGBTARTAB.Open()
					if NOT rsGBTARTAB.EOF then
						If rsGBTARTAB("rul_cod") = "AVT-AUTO" AND rsCons("MSP") <> "" then
							if rsCons("MSP") <= 600000 then
								AVTRate = 0.04
							elseif rsCons("MSP") > 600000 AND rsCons("MSP") <= 1000000 then
								AVTRate = 0.10
							elseif rsCons("MSP") > 1000000 AND rsCons("MSP") <= 4000000 then
								AVTRate = 0.20
							elseif rsCons("MSP") > 4000000 then
								AVTRate = 0.50
							end if
						elseif rsGBTARTAB("rul_cod") = "AVT_HYBRID" AND rsCons("MSP") <> "" then
							if rsCons("MSP") <= 600000 then
								AVTRate = 0.02
							elseif rsCons("MSP") > 600000 AND rsCons("MSP") <= 1000000 then
								AVTRate = 0.05
							elseif rsCons("MSP") > 1000000 AND rsCons("MSP") <= 4000000 then
								AVTRate = 0.10
							elseif rsCons("MSP") > 4000000 then
								AVTRate = 0.25
							end if
						end if
					end if
					
					if rsCons("MSP") <> "" then
						AVTPerItem = ((rsCons("MSP") * AVTRate) * rsCons("SupVal1"))
					else
						AVTPerItem = 0
					end if
					AVTCost = AVTCost + AVTPerItem
					
				End If
				
				'get UOM of AHTN
				set rstUOM = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
				rstUOM.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
				rstUOM.Source = "SELECT IsNull(uom_cod1, '') as uom_cod1 FROM GBTARTAB WHERE hs6_cod = '"& mid(rsCons("HSCode"),1,6) &"' and tar_pr1 = '"& mid(rsCons("HSCode"),7,2) &"'"
				rstUOM.CursorType = 0
				rstUOM.CursorLocation = 2
				rstUOM.LockType = 3
				rstUOM.Open()
				rstUOM_numRows = 0
				
				if NOT rstUOM.EOF then
					EXCUnit = rstUOM("uom_cod1")
				else
					EXCUnit = ""
				end if
				rstUOM.Close()
				
				'Update items
				Set cmdDetailU = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
				cmdDetailU.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
				cmdDetailU.CommandText = "UPDATE TBLIMPAPL_DETAIL Set ExciseType = '"& EXTAX &"', ExciseRate = '"& EXCRate &"', ExciseQty = '"& EXCQty &"', ExciseUnit = '"& EXCUnit &"', ExciseTotal = '"& ExciseTax &"' WHERE ApplNo='" & ApplNumber & "' AND ItemNo = '"& rsCons("ItemNo") &"'"
				cmdDetailU.Execute
				cmdDetailU.ActiveConnection.Close
				
				Set cmdDetailC = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
				cmdDetailC.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
				cmdDetailC.CommandText = "UPDATE TBLIMPAPL_CONS Set ExciseType = '"& EXTAX &"', ExciseRate = '"& EXCRate &"', ExciseQty = '"& EXCQty &"', ExciseUnit = '"& EXCUnit &"', ExciseTotal = '"& ExciseTax &"' WHERE ApplNo='" & ApplNumber & "' AND ItemNo = '"& rsCons("ItemNo") &"'"
				cmdDetailC.Execute
				cmdDetailC.ActiveConnection.Close
				
				rsCons.movenext
			wend
	end if
	
end if

if request.QueryString("ApplNo") <> "" then
	' ApplNumber = request.QueryString("ApplNo")

'CARIE: Validation of Importer TIN v1.0
Function GenerateRandomString(length)
    Randomize
    Dim characters, i, randomString
    characters = "ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ23456789"
    randomString = ""
    For i = 1 To length
        randomString = randomString & Mid(characters, Int((Len(characters) * Rnd) + 1), 1)
    Next
    GenerateRandomString = randomString
End Function

Function StringExistsInTable(randomString)
    Dim conn, cmd, rs, sql
    Set conn = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Connection")
    conn.Open constrCOMINScd1
    sql = "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM CWSEXPORTER WHERE EXP_CODE = '" & randomString & "'"
	
    Set rs = conn.Execute(sql)'
	
    If rs(0) > 0 Then
        StringExistsInTable = True
    Else
        StringExistsInTable = False
    End If
    
    rs.Close
    conn.Close
    Set rs = Nothing
    Set conn = Nothing
End Function
'END CARIE: Validation of Importer TIN v1.0

' *** Insert Record: construct a sql insert statement and execute it
If (CStr(Request("MM_insert")) <> "") Then
	' create the sql insert statement
	MM_tableValues = ""
	MM_dbValues = ""
	For i = LBound(MM_fields) To UBound(MM_fields) Step 2
		FormVal = MM_fields(i+1)
		MM_typeArray = Split(MM_columns(i+1),",")
		Delim = MM_typeArray(0)
		If (Delim = "none") Then Delim = ""
		AltVal = MM_typeArray(1)
		If (AltVal = "none") Then AltVal = ""
		EmptyVal = MM_typeArray(2)
		If (EmptyVal = "none") Then EmptyVal = ""
		If (FormVal = "") Then
			FormVal = EmptyVal
		Else
			If (AltVal <> "") Then
				FormVal = AltVal
			ElseIf (Delim = "'") Then  ' escape quotes
				FormVal = "'" & Replace(FormVal,"'","''") & "'"
			Else
				FormVal = Delim + FormVal + Delim
			End If
		End If
		If (i <> LBound(MM_fields)) Then
			MM_tableValues = MM_tableValues & ","
			MM_dbValues = MM_dbValues & ","
		End if
		MM_tableValues = MM_tableValues & MM_columns(i)
		MM_dbValues = MM_dbValues & FormVal
	Next
	
	'--Opens GBMODTAB Recordset to determine values for MDEC2 and DECDESC.
	Set rstGBMODTAB = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
	'response.write "***" & Session("mod_cod")

	rstGBMODTAB.Source = "SELECT mod_cod, cpl_cod, mod_dsc, ipf, docstamp FROM dbo.GBMODTAB WHERE mod_cod = '" & Session("mod_cod") & "'"
	rstGBMODTAB.CursorType = 0
	rstGBMODTAB.CursorLocation = 2

	rsDetail.CursorLocation = 2
	rsDetail.LockType = 3
	rsDetail.Open
	
	if not rsDetail.EOF then
		strCOrg = rsDetail("CoCode")
	else
		strCOrg = ""
	end if
	intConFlag = 0
	do while not rsDetail.Eof
		if strCOrg <> rsDetail("CoCode") then 
			strCOrg = "MANY"
		end if
		if trim(rsDetail("Cont1")) + trim(rsDetail("Cont2")) + trim(rsDetail("Cont3")) + trim(rsDetail("Cont4")) <> "" then
		intConFlag = 1

	rstTBLIMPAPL.Source = "SELECT *  FROM dbo.TBLIMPAPL_MASTER   WHERE Applno = '" & ApplNumber & "'"
	rstTBLIMPAPL.CursorType = 0

		strDate = ""

		strConName = Request.form("lstConsignee")

		strConAddr2 = Request.form("txtConAddr2")
		strConAddr3 = Request.form("txtConAddr3")
		strConAddr4 = Request.form("txtConAddr4")
    '10142024:SPagara: Enhancement for ASPAC client
    elseif UCase(Session("mod_cod")) = "IES" and isAspacClient = "YES" then

				MM_editQuery = "update dbo.TBLIMPAPL_MASTER Set Mdec='" & rstGBMODTAB("mod_cod") & "', MDec2='" & rstGBMODTAB("cpl_cod") & "', DecDesc='" & Session("DecType") & "', OffClearance='" & strOffName & "', OffClear='" & strOffCode & "', Manifest='" & Replace(Ucase(Request.form("txtManifest")), "'", "''") & "', DtArrv='" & strDate & "', TenRel='" & Ucase(Request.form("txtTenRel")) & "', SupCode='" & Replace(Request.form("txtSuppCode"), "'", "''") & "', SupName='" & Replace(Request.form("lstExporter"), "'", "''") & "', SupAddr1='" & Replace(Request.form("txtSuppAddr1"), "'", "''") & "', SupAddr2='" & Replace(Request.form("txtSuppAddr2"), "'", "''") & "', SupAddr3='" & Replace(Request.form("txtSuppAddr3"), "'", "''") & "', SupAddr4='" & Replace(Request.form("txtSuppAddr4"), "'", "''") & "', BrokerName='" & Replace(Request.form("lstBroker"), "'", "''") & "', BrokAddr1='" & Replace(Request.form("txtBrokAddr1"), "'", "''") & "', BrokAddr2='" & Replace(Request.form("txtBrokAddr2"), "'", "''") & "', BrokAddr3='" & Replace(Request.form("txtBrokAddr3"), "'", "''") & "', DecTin='" & Replace(Request.form("txtDecTin"), "'", "''") & "', Vessel='" & Replace(UCase(Request.form("txtVessel")), "'", "''") & "', RegNo='" & Replace(Ucase(Request.form("txtManifest")), "'", "''") & "', LocalC='" & Replace(UCase(Request.form("txtLocalC")), "'", "''") & "', Cexp='" & Request.form("lstCountry") & "', EntryNumber='" & Replace(Request.form("txtEntryNo"), "'", "''") & "', CRFNo='" & Replace(Request.form("txtCRFNo"), "'", "''") & "', TPort='" & Replace(Request.form("lstTransPort"), "'", "''") & "', PDest='" & Replace(Request.form("lstDestPort"), "'", "''") & "', Lgoods='" & Request.form("lstLGoods") & "', conFlag= " & intConFlag & ", PLoad= '" & Request.form("txtPLoad") & "', Zone= '"& Request.form("lstZone") &"', SchenkerClient= '"& Request.form("SchenkerClient") &"' WHERE ApplNo='" & ApplNumber & "'"
			end if
			
			MM_editQueryExt = "update dbo.TBLIMPAPL_MASTER_EXT Set UConName='"& Request.form("lstUCon") &"', UConAddr1='" & Request.form("txtUConAddr1") & "', UConAddr2='" & Request.form("txtUConAddr2") & "', UConAddr3='" & Request.form("txtUConAddr3") & "', IntRef='" & Request.form("txtIntRef") & "' WHERE ApplNo='" & ApplNumber & "'"
			
			'CARIE: Validation of Importer TIN v1.0
			If UCase(Session("cltcode")) = "FEDEX" and UCase(Session("mod_cod")) <> "IES" Then
			
				'If tin was changed using autocomplete or manual input in txttin
				If request.form("TXTTIN") <> request.form("TXTTIN1") Then
				
					Dim randomString
					Do
						randomString = GenerateRandomString(4)
					Loop While StringExistsInTable(randomString)
					
					'Check the modified consignee tin if existing in cwsexporter
					set rstCopyExporter = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
					rstCopyExporter.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1  
					rstCopyExporter.Source = "SELECT * FROM CWSEXPORTER where EXP_TIN='" & request.form("TXTTIN") & "' and CLTCODE='"& Session("cltcode") &"'"
					rstCopyExporter.CursorType = 0
					rstCopyExporter.CursorLocation = 2
					rstCopyExporter.LockType = 3
					rstCopyExporter.Open
					rstCopyExporter_numRows = 0
					
					'If the inputted tin isn't existing in cwsexporter yet then, insert new in cwsexporter
					If rstCopyExporter.EOF then
						Set rsSearchTIN = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
						rsSearchTIN.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1  
						rsSearchTIN.Source = "SELECT * FROM dbo.uncmptab WHERE CONTIN='" & request.form("TXTTIN") & "'"
						rsSearchTIN.CursorType = 0
						rsSearchTIN.CursorLocation = 2
						rsSearchTIN.LockType = 3
						rsSearchTIN.Open()
						rsSearchTIN_numRows = 0
						
						If Not rsSearchTIN.EOF Then
							MM_editQueryExporter = "INSERT INTO CWSEXPORTER (Exp_code, Exp_name, Exp_TIN, EXP_adr1, Exp_adr2, Exp_adr3, Exp_adr4, ExpDUNs, ExpPlantFaxNo, ExpPlantTelNo, cltcode, date_created, date_modified) VALUES ('" & randomString & "', '" & rsSearchTIN("CONNAME") & "', '" & rsSearchTIN("CONTIN") & "', '" & rsSearchTIN("CONADDR1") & "','" & rsSearchTIN("CONADDR2") & "','" & rsSearchTIN("CONADDR3") & "','" & rsSearchTIN("CONCTY") & "','"&rsSearchTIN("CONTIN")&"','"&rsSearchTIN("CONFAX")&"','"&rsSearchTIN("CONTEL")&"','"& UCase(Session("cltcode")) &"','" & Now() & "','" & Now() & "')"
						End If
					End If
					'Generate new application number 
						Dim DataConnection, cmdDC, cmdDC2, RecordSet, RecordSet2, ApplNo, cntr
				
						Set DataConnection = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Connection")
						DataConnection.Open constrCOMINScdV
					
						Set cmdDC = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
						cmdDC.ActiveConnection = DataConnection
						Set cmdDC2 = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
						cmdDC2.ActiveConnection = DataConnection
					
						cntr = 1
						
						Do While True
						
						set rsCheckExpCode = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
						rsCheckExpCode.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1  
						rsCheckExpCode.Source = "SELECT * FROM CWSEXPORTER where EXP_TIN='" & request.form("TXTTIN") & "' and CLTCODE='"& Session("cltcode") &"'"
						rsCheckExpCode.CursorType = 0
						rsCheckExpCode.CursorLocation = 2
						rsCheckExpCode.LockType = 3
						rsCheckExpCode.Open
						rsCheckExpCode_numRows = 0
						
						If NOT  rsCheckExpCode.EOF Then 'If the tin exist in cwsexporter consignee detail no need to insert
							ApplNoSeries = rsCheckExpCode("Exp_Code")
						Else 'otherwise insert new tin expcode and cltcode
							ApplNoSeries = randomString
						End If
						
						if UCase(Session("cltcode")) = "FEDEX" AND randomString = "IESB" then
							newApplNumber = "IESB" & 3000000 + Trim(CStr(cntr))
						else
							
							if len(randomString) = 3 then
								newApplNumber = ApplNoSeries & Right(CStr(Year(Date)), 2) & Right("00" & Trim(CStr(Month(Date))), 2) & Right("00" & Trim(CStr(Day(Date))), 2) & Right("00" & Trim(CStr(cntr)), 3)
							end if
							if len(randomString) = 4 then
								newApplNumber = ApplNoSeries & Right(CStr(Year(Date)), 1) & Right("00" & Trim(CStr(Month(Date))), 2) & Right("00" & Trim(CStr(Day(Date))), 2) & Right("00" & Trim(CStr(cntr)), 3)
							end if
						end if
						
						SQL2 = "SELECT Applno FROM dbo.TBLIMPAPL_MASTER where APPLNO = '" & Trim(newApplNumber) & "'"
								
							cmdDC2.CommandText = SQL2
							
							Set RecordSet2 = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
							RecordSet2.Open cmdDC2, , 0, 2
							
							If RecordSet2.EOF Then
								Exit Do
							End If
							
							cntr = cntr + 1
						Loop
						
						newApplNumber = Trim(newApplNumber)
						
						set cmd2_appltimer = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
						cmd2_appltimer.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScdV
						cmd2_appltimer.Source="Select applno from dbo.ApplTimer where applno='" & newApplNumber & "'"
						cmd2_appltimer.CursorType = 0
						cmd2_appltimer.CursorLocation = 2
						cmd2_appltimer.LockType = 3
						cmd2_appltimer.Open()
						cmd2_appltimer_numRows = 0

						'Insert to appltimer if no existing applno
						if cmd2_appltimer.eof then
							set cmdApplTIMER = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
							cmdApplTIMER.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd		
							cmdApplTIMER.CommandText = "INSERT INTO dbo.APPLTIMER (ApplNo, cltcode,Screatedate) VALUES ('" & newApplNumber & "','" & Session("cltcode") & "','" & Month(Now) & "/" & Day(Now) & "/" & YEAR(Now) &  " " & Time() & "')"
							cmdApplTIMER.CommandType = 1
							cmdApplTIMER.CommandTimeout = 0
							cmdApplTIMER.Prepared = true
							cmdApplTIMER.Execute()	
							
						else
							set cmdApplTIMER = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
							cmdApplTIMER.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd		
							cmdApplTIMER.CommandText = "UPDATE dbo.APPLTIMER Set SCREATEDATE='" & Month(Now) & "/" & Day(Now) & "/" & YEAR(Now) & " " & Time() & "' WHERE ApplNo='" & newApplNumber & "'"
							cmdApplTIMER.CommandType = 1
							cmdApplTIMER.CommandTimeout = 0
							cmdApplTIMER.Prepared = true
							cmdApplTIMER.Execute()
						End if
						
						strSQLMaster = "insert into dbo.tblimpapl_master (applno, LTOBusinessID, DecTin, MDec, Mdec2, SupName, SupAddr1, SupAddr2, SupAddr3, OffClear, Contin, ConName, ConAddr1, ConAddr2, ConAddr3, ConAddr4, Manifest, ItemCon, Items, Packs, Stat, Vessel, RegNo, LocalC, Tport, Lgoods, CexpDesc, CorgDesc, Cexp, Corg, Cdest, Brokername, BrokAddr1, BrokAddr2, BrokAddr3, ConFlag, REFNO, CRFNO, DoCDATE, SGSFLAG, IAN, TenRel, DtArrv, EntryNumber, TrPermNo, TrBlAwbNo, TrShipCo, TrDepDate, TrTaxAcctNo, TrAddress, TrBrkLicNo, TrPortofOrig, TrPortofDest, TrPortofTrans, CreationDate, DecDesc, OffClearance, PLoad, Zone) select '" & newApplNumber & "', LTOBusinessID, DecTin, MDec, Mdec2, SupName, SupAddr1, SupAddr2, SupAddr3, OffClear, '"&request.form("txtTIN")&"', ConName, ConAddr1, ConAddr2, ConAddr3, ConAddr4, Manifest, ItemCon, Items, Packs, Stat, Vessel, RegNo, LocalC, Tport, Lgoods, CexpDesc, CorgDesc, Cexp, Corg, Cdest, Brokername, BrokAddr1, BrokAddr2, BrokAddr3, ConFlag, REFNO, CRFNO, DoCDATE, SGSFLAG, IAN, TenRel, DtArrv, EntryNumber, TrPermNo, TrBlAwbNo, TrShipCo, TrDepDate, TrTaxAcctNo, TrAddress, TrBrkLicNo, TrPortofOrig, TrPortofDest, TrPortofTrans, '" & Now() & "', DecDesc, OffClearance, PLoad, Zone from tblimpapl_master where applno = '" & ApplNumber & "'"
					
						strSQLMasterExt = "INSERT INTO dbo.TBLIMPAPL_MASTER_EXT (ApplNo, UConName, UConAddr1, UConAddr2, UConAddr3, IntRef) SELECT '" & newApplNumber & "', UConName, UConAddr1, UConAddr2, UConAddr3, IntRef  FROM TBLIMPAPL_MASTER_EXT WHERE ApplNo = '" & ApplNumber & "'"
					
						strSQLDetail = "insert into dbo.tblimpapl_detail (ApplNo, ItemNo, Marks1, Marks2, NoPack, PackCode, Cont1, Cont2, Cont3, Cont4, GoodsDesc, OCharges, IFreight, InvNo, DumpBond, HSCode, HSCODE_TAR, TARSPEC, COCode, ItemGWeight, Pref, ProcDsc, ExtCode, ItemNweight, AirBill, PrevDoc, InvValue, InvCurr, Adjustment, Qty, Unit, gDesc2, gDesc3, SupVal1, SupVal2, SupVal3, SupUnit1, SupUnit2, SupUnit3, ExciseType, ExciseRate, ExciseQty, ExciseUnit, ExciseTotal, HsRate, quo_cod, quo_dsc, ValMethodNum, ValMethodDesc, MSP, Item_uploading_flag) select '" & newApplNumber & "', ItemNo, Marks1, Marks2, NoPack, PackCode, Cont1, Cont2, Cont3, Cont4, GoodsDesc, OCharges, IFreight, InvNo, DumpBond, HSCode, HSCODE_TAR, TARSPEC, COCode, ItemGWeight, Pref, ProcDsc, ExtCode, ItemNweight, AirBill, PrevDoc, InvValue, InvCurr, Adjustment, Qty, Unit, gDesc2, gDesc3, SupVal1, SupVal2, SupVal3, SupUnit1, SupUnit2, SupUnit3, ExciseType, ExciseRate, ExciseQty, ExciseUnit, ExciseTotal, HsRate, quo_cod, quo_dsc, 'NV', 'No Valuation', MSP, Item_uploading_flag from tblimpapl_detail where applno='" & ApplNumber & "'"
					
						strSQLContainer = "insert into dbo.tblimpapl_Container (ApplNo, Container) select '" & newApplNumber & "', Container from tblimpapl_container where applno='" & ApplNumber & "'"
					
						strSQLCons = "insert into dbo.tblimpapl_cons (ApplNo, ItemNo, Marks1, Marks2, NoPack, PackCode, Cont1, Cont2, Cont3, Cont4, GoodsDesc, OCharges, IFreight, InvNo, DumpBond, HSCode, HSCODE_TAR, TARSPEC, COCode, ItemGWeight, Pref, ProcDsc, ExtCode, ItemNweight, AirBill, PrevDoc, InvValue, InvCurr, Adjustment, Qty, Unit, gDesc2, gDesc3, SupVal1, SupVal2, SupVal3, SupUnit1, SupUnit2, SupUnit3, ExciseType, ExciseRate, ExciseQty, ExciseUnit, ExciseTotal, hsrate, quo_cod, quo_dsc, ValMethodNum, ValMethodDesc, MSP, Item_uploading_flag) select '" & newApplNumber & "', ItemNo, Marks1, Marks2, NoPack, PackCode, Cont1, Cont2, Cont3, Cont4, GoodsDesc, OCharges, IFreight, InvNo, DumpBond, HSCode, HSCODE_TAR, TARSPEC, COCode, ItemGWeight, Pref, ProcDsc, ExtCode, ItemNweight, AirBill, PrevDoc, InvValue, InvCurr, Adjustment, Qty, Unit, gDesc2, gDesc3, SupVal1, SupVal2, SupVal3, SupUnit1, SupUnit2, SupUnit3, ExciseType, ExciseRate, ExciseQty, ExciseUnit, ExciseTotal, hsrate, quo_cod, quo_dsc, 'NV', 'No Valuation', MSP, Item_uploading_flag from tblimpapl_cons where applno='" & ApplNumber & "'"

						set rstExchRate = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
						rstExchRate.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScdV

						rstExchRate.CursorType = 0

						rstExchRate.Close
					
						strSQLFin = "insert into dbo.tblimpapl_fin (ApplNo, TDelivery, TPaymentDesc, Tpayment, BankName, BankCode, BranchCode, BankRef, CustomVal, CustCurr, FreightCost, FreightCurr, WharCost, WharCurr, InsCost, InsCurr, OtherCost, OtherCurr, ArrasCost, ArrasCurr, WareCode, WareDelay, WOBankCharge, EXCHRATE, PrepAcct, IntRef, IEDno, TCCno, TDMno, IEDno1, TCCno1, TDMno1, IEDno2, TCCno2, TDMno2, PolicyNo) select '" & newApplNumber & "', TDelivery, TPaymentDesc, Tpayment, BankName, BankCode, BranchCode, BankRef, CustomVal, CustCurr, FreightCost, FreightCurr, WharCost, WharCurr, InsCost, InsCurr, OtherCost, OtherCurr, ArrasCost, ArrasCurr, WareCode, WareDelay, WOBankCharge, '" & ExchRate & "', PrepAcct, IntRef, IEDno, TCCno, TDMno, IEDno1, TCCno1, TDMno1, IEDno2, TCCno2, TDMno2, PolicyNo from tblimpapl_fin where applno='" & ApplNumber & "'"
						
				End If
			End IF
			'End CARIE: Validation of Importer TIN v1.0
			
		end if
		Session("Query") = MM_editQuery
		
	End If
  
	rstTBLIMPAPL.Close
	If UCase(Session("cltcode")) = "FEDEX" AND UCase(Session("mod_cod")) = "IES" then
		'LObligado Activity Logs
		MM_editQueryLogs = "IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT * FROM TBLIMPAPL_LOGS WHERE APPLNO='" &ApplNumber& "' AND ConName='"&strConName&"' AND ConAddr1='"&strConAddr1&"' AND ConAddr2='"&strConAddr2&"' AND ConAddr3='"&strConAddr3&"' AND ConAddr4 = '"&strConAddr4&"' AND MDec = '"&rstGBMODTAB("Mod_Cod")&"' AND Pdest='"&Request.form("lstDestPort")&"' AND Lgoods='"&Request.form("lstLGoods")&"' AND Cexp='"&Request.form("lstCountry")&"' AND LocalC='"&Request.form("txtLocalC")&"' AND DateModified='"&now()&"') BEGIN INSERT INTO " & MM_editTable3 & " (dtarrv, LGoods, DateModified, ApplNo, MDec, MDec2, DecDesc, OffClear, OffClearance, Stat, conFlag,PLoad, Zone, ConName, ConAddr1, ConAddr2, ConAddr3, ConAddr4, UserName, " & MM_tableValues & ") VALUES ('" & strDate & "','" & Request.form("lstLGoods") & "', '" & Now() & "','" & ApplNumber & "', '" & rstGBMODTAB("Mod_Cod") & "', '" & rstGBMODTAB("Cpl_Cod") & "', '" & Session("DecType") & "', '" & strOffCode & "', '" & strOffName & "', '" & strStatus & "', " & intConFlag & ", '"& Request.form("txtPLoad") &"', '"& Request.form("lstZone") &"', '" & strConName & "', '" & strConAddr1 & "', '" & strConAddr2 & "', '" & strConAddr3 & "', '" & strConAddr4 & "', '" & Session("UserID") & "'," & MM_dbValues & "); END" 'If there's additional condtion, add "ELSE BEGIN END"

		set rstPrevLogs = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
		rstPrevLogs.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1    
		rstPrevLogs.Source = "SELECT *  FROM dbo.TBLIMPAPL_PREVIOUSLOGS WHERE Applno = '" & ApplNumber & "'"
		rstPrevLogs.CursorType = 0
		rstPrevLogs.CursorLocation = 2
		rstPrevLogs.LockType = 3
		rstPrevLogs.Open()
		rstPrevLogs_numRows = 0
	
		IF NOT rstPrevLogs.EOF THEN

			set rstCopyLogs = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
			rstCopyLogs.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1  
			rstCopyLogs.Source = "SELECT TOP 1 * FROM TBLIMPAPL_LOGS where APPLNO='" &ApplNumber& "' and DecTin!='' ORDER BY datemodified DESC"
			rstCopyLogs.CursorType = 0
			rstCopyLogs.CursorLocation = 2
			rstCopyLogs.LockType = 3
			rstCopyLogs.Open
			rstCopyLogs_numRows = 0

			If not rstCopyLogs.eof then
				MM_editQueryPreviousLogs = "IF NOT EXISTS (SELECT * FROM TBLIMPAPL_PREVIOUSLOGS WHERE APPLNO='" &ApplNumber& "' AND ConName='"&strConName&"' AND ConAddr1='"&strConAddr1&"' AND ConAddr2='"&strConAddr2&"' AND ConAddr3='"&strConAddr3&"' AND ConAddr4 = '"&strConAddr4&"' AND MDec = '"&rstGBMODTAB("Mod_Cod")&"' AND Pdest='"&Request.form("lstDestPort")&"' AND Lgoods='"&Request.form("lstLGoods")&"' AND Cexp='"&Request.form("lstCountry")&"' AND LocalC='"&Request.form("txtLocalC")&"' AND datemodified='"&now()&"') BEGIN INSERT INTO " & MM_editTable4 & " ( ApplNo, DateModified, DecTin, MDec, Mdec2, SupName, SupAddr1, SupAddr2, SupAddr3, OffClear, ConTIN, Manifest, ItemCon, Items, Packs, Stat, Vessel, RegNo, LocalC, Tport, Pdest, Lgoods, CexpDesc, CorgDesc, Cexp, Corg, Cdest, Brokername, BrokAddr1, BrokAddr2, BrokAddr3, ConFlag, REFNO, CRFNO, DoCDATE, SGSFLAG, IAN, TenRel, DtArrv, EntryNumber, TrPermNo, TrBlAwbNo, TrShipCo, TrDepDate, TrTaxAcctNo, TrAddress, TrBrkLicNo, TrPortofOrig, TrPortofDest, TrPortofTrans, CreationDate, DecDesc, OffClearance, Environment, SentDate, PLoad, UserName, [Zone], SPSFrom, MAVICFrom, CodeLen, PEZANo, Filename1, ConName, ConAddr1, ConAddr2, ConAddr3, SupAddr4, isFedex, hasTransfer, [Filename], LTOBusinessID, ConAddr4) VALUES ('" & ApplNumber & "', '"&Now()&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("DecTin")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("MDec")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("Mdec2")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("SupName")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("SupAddr1")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("SupAddr2")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("SupAddr3")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("OffClear")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("ConTIN")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("Manifest")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("ItemCon")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("Items")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("Packs")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("Stat")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("Vessel")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("RegNo")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("LocalC")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("Tport")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("Pdest")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("Lgoods")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("CexpDesc")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("CorgDesc")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("Cexp")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("Corg")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("Cdest")&"', '"&rstCopyLogs("Brokername")&"', 	rstGBMODTAB.Close
	
	Set rstGBMODTAB = Nothing
	Set rstTBLIMPAPL = Nothing
	
	If (Not MM_abortEdit) Then
		' execute the insert
		Set MM_editCmdExt = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
		MM_editCmdExt.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1  	
		MM_editCmdExt.CommandText = MM_editQueryExt
		MM_editCmdExt.Execute
		
		MM_editCmdExt.ActiveConnection.Close

			If request.form("TXTTIN") = request.form("TXTTIN1") Then
				Set MM_editCmd = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
				MM_editCmd.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1  	
				MM_editCmd.CommandText = MM_editQuery
				MM_editCmd.Execute
				MM_editCmd.ActiveConnection.Close
			End If
		Else
			Set MM_editCmd = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
			MM_editCmd.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1  	
			MM_editCmd.CommandText = MM_editQuery
			MM_editCmd.Execute
			MM_editCmd.ActiveConnection.Close
		End If

		if UCase(Session("cltcode")) = "FEDEX" AND UCase(Session("mod_cod")) = "IES" then
			''LObligado Activity Logs
			Set MM_editCmdLogs = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
			MM_editCmdLogs.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1  
			MM_editCmdLogs.CommandText = MM_editQueryLogs
			MM_editCmdLogs.Execute
			MM_editCmdLogs.ActiveConnection.Close

			' FOR PREVIOUS LOGS
			Set MM_editCmdPrevLogs = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
			MM_editCmdPrevLogs.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1  
			MM_editCmdPrevLogs.CommandText = MM_editQueryPreviousLogs
			MM_editCmdPrevLogs.Execute
			MM_editCmdPrevLogs.ActiveConnection.Close
		End If
		
		' CARIE: Validation of Importer TIN v1.0 - cltcode:
		If UCase(Session("cltcode")) = "FEDEX" and UCase(Session("mod_cod")) <> "IES" Then'
			If request.form("TXTTIN") <> request.form("TXTTIN1") then
				'Check the modified consignee tin if existing in cwsexporter
				set rstCopyExporter = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
				rstCopyExporter.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1  
				rstCopyExporter.Source = "SELECT * FROM CWSEXPORTER where EXP_TIN='" & request.form("TXTTIN") & "' and CLTCODE='"& Session("cltcode") &"'"
				rstCopyExporter.CursorType = 0
				rstCopyExporter.CursorLocation = 2
				rstCopyExporter.LockType = 3
				rstCopyExporter.Open
				rstCopyExporter_numRows = 0
				
				'If the inputted tin isn't existing in cwsexporter yet then, insert new in cwsexporter
				If rstCopyExporter.EOF then
					Set rsSearchTIN = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
					rsSearchTIN.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1  
					rsSearchTIN.Source = "SELECT * FROM dbo.uncmptab WHERE CONTIN='" & request.form("TXTTIN") & "'"
					rsSearchTIN.CursorType = 0
					rsSearchTIN.CursorLocation = 2
					rsSearchTIN.LockType = 3
					rsSearchTIN.Open()
					rsSearchTIN_numRows = 0
					
					If Not rsSearchTIN.EOF Then		
						Set MM_editCmdExporter = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
						MM_editCmdExporter.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1  	
						MM_editCmdExporter.CommandText = MM_editQueryExporter
						MM_editCmdExporter.Execute
						MM_editCmdExporter.ActiveConnection.Close
					End If
				End If
				
				' MASTER
					set cmdInsertMaster = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
					cmdInsertMaster.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd
					cmdInsertMaster.CommandText = strSQLMaster
					cmdInsertMaster.CommandType = 1
					cmdInsertMaster.CommandTimeout = 0
					cmdInsertMaster.Prepared = true
					cmdInsertMaster.Execute()	
					
					' MASTER EXTENSION
					set cmdInsertMasterExt = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
					cmdInsertMasterExt.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd
					cmdInsertMasterExt.CommandText = strSQLMasterExt
					cmdInsertMasterExt.CommandType = 1
					cmdInsertMasterExt.CommandTimeout = 0
					cmdInsertMasterExt.Prepared = true
					cmdInsertMasterExt.Execute()
					
					' ITEM DETAIL
					set cmdInsertItemDetail = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
					cmdInsertItemDetail.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd		
					cmdInsertItemDetail.CommandText = strSQLDetail
					cmdInsertItemDetail.CommandType = 1
					cmdInsertItemDetail.CommandTimeout = 0
					cmdInsertItemDetail.Prepared = true
					cmdInsertItemDetail.Execute()	
			
					' CONTAINER
					set cmdInsertContainer = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
					cmdInsertContainer.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd
					cmdInsertContainer.CommandText = strSQLContainer
					cmdInsertContainer.CommandType = 1
					cmdInsertContainer.CommandTimeout = 0
					cmdInsertContainer.Prepared = true
					cmdInsertContainer.Execute()	
					
					' CONSOLIDATED
					set cmdInsertConsolidated = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
					cmdInsertConsolidated.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd		
					cmdInsertConsolidated.CommandText = strSQLCons
					cmdInsertConsolidated.CommandType = 1
					cmdInsertConsolidated.CommandTimeout = 0
					cmdInsertConsolidated.Prepared = true
					cmdInsertConsolidated.Execute()	
					
					' FINACIAL
					set cmdInsertFinancial = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
					cmdInsertFinancial.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd		
					cmdInsertFinancial.CommandText = strSQLFin
					cmdInsertFinancial.CommandType = 1
					cmdInsertFinancial.CommandTimeout = 0
					cmdInsertFinancial.Prepared = true
					cmdInsertFinancial.Execute()	
					
					Response.Redirect("cws_impdec.asp?ApplNo="& newApplNumber &"&status="& Stats &"")
			End If
		End If
		'END CARIE: Validation of Importer TIN v1.0 - cltcode:
		
		If (MM_editRedirectUrl <> "") Then
			Response.Redirect(MM_editRedirectUrl)
		End If
	End If
End If

			rsLogsF.Source = "SELECT * from dbo.tblIMPApl_Fin WHERE ApplNo= '" & ApplNumber & "'"
			
			rsLogsF.CursorType = 0
			rsLogsF.CursorLocation = 2
			rsLogsF.LockType = 3
			rsLogsF.Open
			rsLogsF_numRows = 0
			
			if not rsLogsF.EOF Then
				set cmdInsert1 = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
				cmdInsert1.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1

				cmdInsert1.CommandText = "INSERT INTO dbo.tblimpapl_logs (ApplNo, TDelivery, TPaymentDesc, Tpayment, BankName, BankCode, BranchCode, CustomVal, CustCurr, FreightCost, FreightCurr, WharCost, WharCurr, InsCost, InsCurr, OtherCost, OtherCurr, ArrasCost, ArrasCurr, WareCode, WareDelay, WOBankCharge, EXCHRATE, PrepAcct, IntRef) VALUES ('" & ApplNumber & "','" & rsLogsF("TDelivery") & "','" & rsLogsF("TPaymentDesc") & "','" & rsLogsF("TPayment") & "','" & rsLogsF("BankName") & "','" & rsLogsF("BankCode") & "','" & rsLogsF("BranchCode") & "','" & rsLogsF("CustomVal") & "','" & rsLogsF("CustCurr") & "','" & FormatNumber(rsLogsF("FreightCost"),2) & "','" & rsLogsF("FreightCurr") & "', '" & FormatNumber(rsLogsF("WharCost"),2) & "', '" & rsLogsF("WharCurr") & "', '" & FormatNumber(rsLogsF("InsCost"),2) & "', '" & rsLogsF("InsCurr") & "', '" & FormatNumber(rsLogsF("OtherCost"),2) & "', '" & rsLogsF("OtherCurr") & "', '" & FormatNumber(rsLogsF("ArrasCost"),2) & "', '" & rsLogsF("ArrasCurr") & "', '" & rsLogsF("WareCode") & "', '" & rsLogsF("WareDelay") & "', '" & rsLogsF("WOBankCharge") & "', '" & rsLogsF("ExchRate") & "', '" & rsLogsF("PrepAcct") & "', '" & rsLogsF("IntRef") & "')"
					
				cmdInsert1.CommandType = 1
				cmdInsert1.CommandTimeout = 0
				cmdInsert1.Prepared = true

				cmdInsert1PrevFin.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1			
				cmdInsert1PrevFin.CommandText = "INSERT INTO dbo.TBLIMPAPL_PREVIOUSLOGS (ApplNo, TDelivery, TPaymentDesc, Tpayment, BankName, BankCode, BranchCode, CustomVal, CustCurr, FreightCost, FreightCurr, WharCost, WharCurr, InsCost, InsCurr, OtherCost, OtherCurr, ArrasCost, ArrasCurr, WareCode, WareDelay, WOBankCharge, EXCHRATE, PrepAcct, IntRef) VALUES ('" & ApplNumber & "','" & rsLogsF("TDelivery") & "','" & rsLogsF("TPaymentDesc") & "','" & rsLogsF("TPayment") & "','" & rsLogsF("BankName") & "','" & rsLogsF("BankCode") & "','" & rsLogsF("BranchCode") & "','" & rsLogsF("CustomVal") & "','" & rsLogsF("CustCurr") & "','" & FormatNumber(rsLogsF("FreightCost"),2) & "','" & rsLogsF("FreightCurr") & "', '" & FormatNumber(rsLogsF("WharCost"),2) & "', '" & rsLogsF("WharCurr") & "', '" & FormatNumber(rsLogsF("InsCost"),2) & "', '" & rsLogsF("InsCurr") & "', '" & FormatNumber(rsLogsF("OtherCost"),2) & "', '" & rsLogsF("OtherCurr") & "', '" & FormatNumber(rsLogsF("ArrasCost"),2) & "', '" & rsLogsF("ArrasCurr") & "', '" & rsLogsF("WareCode") & "', '" & rsLogsF("WareDelay") & "', '" & rsLogsF("WOBankCharge") & "', '" & rsLogsF("ExchRate") & "', '" & rsLogsF("PrepAcct") & "', '" & rsLogsF("IntRef") & "')"

				fedexTin = rsCheckUncmptab("contin")

			End If

		end If
		
		rsCheckUncmptab.Close
		Set rsCheckUncmptab = Nothing
	End If

function show_calendar(str_target, str_datetime) {
	var arr_months = ["January", "February", "March", "April", "May", "June",
		"July", "August", "September", "October", "November", "December"];
	var week_days = ["Su", "Mo", "Tu", "We", "Th", "Fr", "Sa"];
	var n_weekstart = 1; // day week starts from (normally 0 or 1)

	var dt_datetime = (str_datetime == null || str_datetime =="" ?  new Date() : new Date(str_datetime));
	var dt_prev_month = new Date(dt_datetime);
	dt_prev_month.setMonth(dt_datetime.getMonth()-1);
	var dt_next_month = new Date(dt_datetime);
	dt_next_month.setMonth(dt_datetime.getMonth()+1);
	var dt_firstday = new Date(dt_datetime);
	dt_firstday.setDate(1);
	dt_firstday.setDate(1-(7+dt_firstday.getDay()-n_weekstart)%7);
	var dt_lastday = new Date(dt_next_month);
	dt_lastday.setDate(0);
	
	// html generation (feel free to tune it for your particular application)
	// print calendar header
	var str_buffer = new String (
		"<html>\n"+
		"<head>\n"+
		"	<title>Calendar</title>\n"+
		"</head>\n"+
		"<body bgcolor=\"White\">\n"+
		"<table class=\"clsOTable\" cellspacing=\"0\" border=\"0\" width=\"100%\">\n"+
		"<tr><td bgcolor=\"#4682B4\">\n"+
		"<table cellspacing=\"1\" cellpadding=\"3\" border=\"0\" width=\"100%\">\n"+
		"<tr>\n	<td bgcolor=\"#4682B4\"><a href=\"javascript:window.opener.show_calendar('"+
		str_target+"', '"+ dt2dtstr(dt_prev_month)+"'+document.cal.time.value);\">"+
		"<img src=\"prev.gif\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" border=\"0\""+
		" alt=\"previous month\"></a></td>\n"+
		"	<td bgcolor=\"#4682B4\" colspan=\"5\">"+
		"<font color=\"white\" face=\"tahoma, verdana\" size=\"2\">"
		+arr_months[dt_datetime.getMonth()]+" "+dt_datetime.getFullYear()+"</font></td>\n"+
		"	<td bgcolor=\"#4682B4\" align=\"right\"><a href=\"javascript:window.opener.show_calendar('"
		+str_target+"', '"+dt2dtstr(dt_next_month)+"'+document.cal.time.value);\">"+
		"<img src=\"next.gif\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" border=\"0\""+
		" alt=\"next month\"></a></td>\n</tr>\n"
	);

	var dt_current_day = new Date(dt_firstday);
	// print weekdays titles
	str_buffer += "<tr>\n";
	for (var n=0; n<7; n++)
		str_buffer += "	<td bgcolor=\"#87CEFA\">"+
		"<font color=\"white\" face=\"tahoma, verdana\" size=\"2\">"+
		week_days[(n_weekstart+n)%7]+"</font></td>\n";
	// print calendar table
	str_buffer += "</tr>\n";
	while (dt_current_day.getMonth() == dt_datetime.getMonth() ||
		dt_current_day.getMonth() == dt_firstday.getMonth()) {
		// print row heder
		str_buffer += "<tr>\n";
		for (var n_current_wday=0; n_current_wday<7; n_current_wday++) {
				if (dt_current_day.getDate() == dt_datetime.getDate() &&
					dt_current_day.getMonth() == dt_datetime.getMonth())
					// print current date
					str_buffer += "	<td bgcolor=\"#FFB6C1\" align=\"right\">";
				else if (dt_current_day.getDay() == 0 || dt_current_day.getDay() == 6)
					// weekend days
					str_buffer += "	<td bgcolor=\"#DBEAF5\" align=\"right\">";
				else
					// print working days of current month
					str_buffer += "	<td bgcolor=\"white\" align=\"right\">";

				if (dt_current_day.getMonth() == dt_datetime.getMonth())
					// print days of current month
					str_buffer += "<a href=\"javascript:window.opener."+str_target+
					".value='"+dt2dtstr(dt_current_day)+"'+document.cal.time.value; window.close();\">"+
					"<font color=\"black\" face=\"tahoma, verdana\" size=\"2\">";
				else 
					// print days of other months
					str_buffer += "<a href=\"javascript:window.opener."+str_target+
					".value='"+dt2dtstr(dt_current_day)+"'+document.cal.time.value; window.close();\">"+
					"<font color=\"gray\" face=\"tahoma, verdana\" size=\"2\">";
				str_buffer += dt_current_day.getDate()+"</font></a></td>\n";
				dt_current_day.setDate(dt_current_day.getDate()+1);
		}
		// print row footer
		str_buffer += "</tr>\n";
	}
	// print calendar footer
    str_buffer +=
        "<form name=\"cal\">\n<tr><td colspan=\"7\" bgcolor=\"#87CEFA\">" +
        "<input type=\"hidden\" name=\"time\" </font></td></tr>\n</form>\n" +
        "</table>\n" +
        "</tr>\n</td>\n</table>\n" +
        "</body>\n" +
        "</html>\n";

    var vWinCal = window.open("", "Calendar",
        "width=200,height=200,status=no,resizable=no,top=200,left=200");
	vWinCal.opener = self;
	var calc_doc = vWinCal.document;
	calc_doc.write (str_buffer);
	calc_doc.close();
}
// Carie: 06072023: IES Lodgement Concerns / Back and Forward Button in Flight Date
function dt2dtstr(dt_datetime) {
    return (
        dt_datetime.getFullYear() + "-" +
        (dt_datetime.getMonth() + 1).toString().padStart(2, "0") + "-" +
        dt_datetime.getDate().toString().padStart(2, "0")
    );
}

function MM_swapImgRestore() { //v3.0
  var i,x,a=document.MM_sr; for(i=0;a&&i<a.length&&(x=a[i])&&x.oSrc;i++) x.src=x.oSrc;
}

function MM_preloadImages() { //v3.0
  var d=document; if(d.images){ if(!d.MM_p) d.MM_p=new Array();
    var i,j=d.MM_p.length,a=MM_preloadImages.arguments; for(i=0; i<a.length; i++)
    if (a[i].indexOf("#")!=0){ d.MM_p[j]=new Image; d.MM_p[j++].src=a[i];}}
}

function MM_swapImage() { //v3.0
  var i,j=0,x,a=MM_swapImage.arguments; document.MM_sr=new Array; for(i=0;i<(a.length-2);i+=3)
   if ((x=MM_findObj(a[i]))!=null){document.MM_sr[j++]=x; if(!x.oSrc) x.oSrc=x.src; x.src=a[i+2];}
}

function MM_findObj(n, d) { //v4.01
  var p,i,x;  if(!d) d=document; if((p=n.indexOf("?"))>0&&parent.frames.length) {
    d=parent.frames[n.substring(p+1)].document; n=n.substring(0,p);}
  if(!(x=d[n])&&d.all) x=d.all[n]; for (i=0;!x&&i<d.forms.length;i++) x=d.forms[i][n];
  for(i=0;!x&&d.layers&&i<d.layers.length;i++) x=MM_findObj(n,d.layers[i].document);
  if(!x && d.getElementById) x=d.getElementById(n); return x;
}

</SCRIPT>

							Set MM_updateSec = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
							MM_updateSec.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1  	
							MM_updateSec.CommandText = "UPDATE tblIMPAPL_Detail SET Section='" & rstSect1("section") & "' WHERE applno = '"& ApplNumber &"' AND itemno = '"& rstSectionn("itemno") &"'"
							MM_updateSec.Execute
															
							MM_updateSec.ActiveConnection.Close
							rstSect1.Close
							rstSectionn.movenext
						wend
						rstSectionn.Close
					
						'cleanup
						set rstDEL = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
						rstDEL.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1						
						rstDEL.CommandText="DELETE FROM tblST WHERE ApplNo='"& ApplNumber &"'"
						rstDEL.Execute
						
						
						'check single
						set rstSection1 = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
						rstSection1.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1												
						rstSection1.Source="SELECT invvalue, hsrate, hscode+hscode_tar as hscod FROM tblimpapl_detail WHERE applno='"& ApplNumber &"' ORDER BY ItemNo"
						rstSection1.CursorType = 0
						rstSection1.CursorLocation = 2
						rstSection1.LockType = 3
						rstSection1.Open()
						rstSection1_numRows = 0
						
						if NOT rstSection1.EOF then
							
							while NOT rstSection1.EOF
								set rstSection3 = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
								rstSection3.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
								if mid(rstSection1("hscod"),1,2) = "84" then
									rstSection3.Source="SELECT section FROM tblSectionFAN WHERE ASEAN = '" & mid(rstSection1("hscod"),1,4) & "'"
								else
									rstSection3.Source="SELECT section FROM tblSectionFAN WHERE ASEAN = '" & mid(rstSection1("hscod"),1,2) & "'"
								end if
								rstSection3.CursorType = 0
								rstSection3.CursorLocation = 2
								rstSection3.LockType = 3
								rstSection3.Open()
								rstSection3_numRows = 0
								
								set rstSection4 = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
								rstSection4.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1						
								rstSection4.Source="SELECT * FROM tblST WHERE sect='"& rstSection3("section") &"' AND ApplNo='"& ApplNumber &"'"
								rstSection4.CursorType = 0
								rstSection4.CursorLocation = 2
								rstSection4.LockType = 3
								rstSection4.Open()
								rstSection4_numRows = 0
								
								if rstSection4.EOF then
									Set MM_insert = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
									MM_insert.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1  	
									MM_insert.CommandText = "INSERT INTO tblST (ApplNo, Sect, TVal, OVal) values ('"& ApplNumber &"', '"  & rstSection3("section") & "', '" & rstSection1("InvValue") & "','" & rstSection1("InvValue") & "')"
									MM_insert.Execute
											
									MM_insert.ActiveConnection.Close						
								else
									TInv = rstSection4("TVal") + rstSection1("invvalue")
										
									Set MM_update = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
									MM_update.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1  	
									MM_update.CommandText = "UPDATE tblST SET TVal='" & cdbl(TInv) & "' WHERE sect = '"& rstSection4("sect") &"' AND ApplNo='"& ApplNumber &"'"
									MM_update.Execute
												
									MM_update.ActiveConnection.Close									
								end if
								rstSection3.Close
								rstSection4.Close
								rstSection1.movenext
							wend
						end if
						rstSection1.Close
						
						'second pass: highest hs rate value
						set rstSection10 = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
						rstSection10.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
						rstSection10.Source="SELECT TOP (1) tval, count(tval) as ctval FROM tblST WHERE applno='"& ApplNumber &"' GROUP BY tval HAVING (count(tval) > 0) ORDER BY CONVERT(FLOAT, REPLACE(tval, CHAR(0), '0')) DESC"
						rstSection10.CursorType = 0
						rstSection10.CursorLocation = 2
						rstSection10.LockType = 3
						rstSection10.Open()
						rstSection10_numRows = 0
						
						if cint(rstSection10("ctval")) < 2 then
							set rstSection11 = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
							rstSection11.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
							rstSection11.Source="SELECT sect FROM tblST WHERE applno='"& ApplNumber &"' AND Tval='"& rstSection10("tval")&"'"
							rstSection11.CursorType = 0
							rstSection11.CursorLocation = 2
							rstSection11.LockType = 3
							rstSection11.Open()
							rstSection11_numRows = 0
											
							response.write "Section: " & rstSection11("sect")
							Session("Secti") = rstSection11("sect")
							rstSection11.Close
							'end of process							
						else
							set rstSection12 = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
							rstSection12.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
							rstSection12.Source="SELECT distinct sect FROM tblST WHERE applno='"& ApplNumber &"' AND Tval='"& rstSection10("tval")&"' ORDER BY sect DESC"				
							rstSection12.CursorType = 0
							rstSection12.CursorLocation = 2
							rstSection12.LockType = 3
							rstSection12.Open()
							rstSection12_numRows = 0
							
							'cleanup
							set rstDEL = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
							rstDEL.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1						
							rstDEL.CommandText="DELETE FROM tblSR WHERE ApplNo='"& ApplNumber &"'"
							rstDEL.Execute
							
							while NOT rstSection12.EOF
								set rstSection13 = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
								rstSection13.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
								rstSection13.Source="SELECT Section, hsrate, hscode + hscode_tar as hscod FROM tblIMPAPL_detail WHERE applno='"& ApplNumber &"' AND Section='"& rstSection12("sect")&"' order by hsrate desc, hscode + hscode_tar desc"											
								rstSection13.CursorType = 0
								rstSection13.CursorLocation = 2
								rstSection13.LockType = 3
								rstSection13.Open()

									rstSection13hsrate = rstSection13("hsrate")
									rstSection13hscod = rstSection13("hscod")
								else
									rstSection13hsrate = ""
									rstSection13hscod = ""
								end if
								
								while NOT rstSection13.EOF								
									Set MM_insertR8 = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
									MM_insertR8.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1  	
									MM_insertR8.CommandText = "INSERT INTO tblSR (ApplNo, Sect, hsr8, hscod) values ('"& ApplNumber &"', '"  & rstSection12("sect") & "', '" & rstSection13hsrate & "','" & rstSection13hscod  & "')"
									MM_insertR8.Execute
											
									MM_insertR8.ActiveConnection.Close
									
									rstSection13.movenext
								wend
								rstSection13.Close
								rstSection12.movenext
							wend
							rstSection12.Close
							
							'third pass: highest gross weight
							set rstSection14 = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
							rstSection14.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
							rstSection14.Source="SELECT TOP (1) hsr8, count(hsr8) as thsr8 FROM tblSR WHERE applno='"& ApplNumber &"' GROUP BY hsr8 HAVING (count(hsr8) > 0) ORDER BY CONVERT(INT, REPLACE(hsr8, CHAR(0), '0')) DESC"
							rstSection14.CursorType = 0
							rstSection14.CursorLocation = 2
							rstSection14.LockType = 3
							rstSection14.Open()
							rstSection14_numRows = 0							
							
							if cint(rstSection14("thsr8")) < 2 then
								set rstSection15 = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
								rstSection15.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
								rstSection15.Source="SELECT sect FROM tblSR WHERE applno='"& ApplNumber &"' AND hsr8='"& rstSection14("hsr8")&"'"
								rstSection15.CursorType = 0
								rstSection15.CursorLocation = 2
								rstSection15.LockType = 3
								rstSection15.Open()
								rstSection15_numRows = 0
								
								if not rstSection15.eof then
									rstSection15sect = rstSection15("sect")
								else
									rstSection15sect = ""
								end if
								response.write "Section: " & rstSection15("sect")
								Session("Secti") = rstSection15("sect")
								rstSection15.Close
								'end of process

								set rstSection16 = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
								rstSection16.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1

									set rstSection17 = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
									rstSection17.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
									rstSection17.Source="SELECT Section, itemgweight, hscode + hscode_tar as hscod FROM tblIMPAPL_detail WHERE applno='"& ApplNumber &"' AND Section='"& rstSection16sect&"' order by itemgweight desc, hscode + hscode_tar desc"											
									rstSection17.CursorType = 0
									rstSection17.CursorLocation = 2
									rstSection17.LockType = 3
									rstSection17.Open()
									rstSection17_numRows = 0
									
									if not rstSection17.eof then
										rstSection17hscod = rstSection17("hscod")
										rstSection17itemgweight = rstSection17("itemgweight")
									else
										rstSection17hscod = ""
										rstSection17itemgweight = ""
									end if 
									
									while NOT rstSection17.EOF								
										Set MM_insertR9 = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Command")
										MM_insertR9.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1  	
										MM_insertR9.CommandText = "INSERT INTO tblSG (ApplNo, Sect, gweight, hscod) values ('"& ApplNumber &"', '"  & rstSection16sect & "', '" & rstSection17itemgweight & "','" & rstSection17hscod  & "')"
												
										MM_insertR9.ActiveConnection.Close

									wend
									rstSection17.Close
									rstSection16.movenext
								wend
								rstSection16.Close
								
								'last pass: highest AHTN
								set rstSection18 = Server.CreateObject("ADODB.Recordset")
								rstSection18.ActiveConnection = constrCOMINScd1
								rstSection18.Source="SELECT TOP (1) gweight, count(isnull(gweight, '0')) as tgweight FROM tblSG WHERE applno='"& ApplNumber &"' GROUP BY gweight HAVING (count(gweight) > 0) ORDER BY CONVERT(FLOAT, REPLACE(gweight, CHAR(0), '0')) DESC"
								rstSection18.CursorType = 0
								rstSection18.CursorLocation = 2
								rstSection18.LockType = 3
								rstSection18.Open()

										rstSection19.CursorType = 0

										rstSection20.Source="SELECT TOP 1 sect FROM tblSG WHERE applno='"& ApplNumber &"' AND gweight='"& rstSection18("gweight")&"' ORDER BY hscod DESC"
										rstSection20.CursorType = 0

										rstSection20.LockType = 3
										rstSection20.Open()
										rstSection20_numRows = 0
										
										response.write "Section: " & rstSection20("sect")
										Session("Secti") = rstSection20("sect")
										rstSection20.Close
										'end of process
									end if
								rstSection18.Close
								end if
							end if
							rstSection14.Close
						end if
						rstSection10.Close	
					
					else
						if ItemsCheck <> "" then
							response.write "<font color='Darkred' size='4'> Items with Invalid HS Code:" & ItemsCheck & "</font>"
						end if

<script type="text/javascript" defer>
<%If UCASE(Session("CLTCODE")) = "FEDEX" AND (Ucase(Session("mod_cod")) = "8ZN" OR Ucase(Session("mod_cod"))="8ZE") then%>	
	function searchDatabase() {
	  var xmlhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();
	  var url = "cws_impdecSearchPdest.asp";
	  var pdest = document.getElementById("lstDestPortName").value;
	  
	  url += "?pdest=" + pdest;
	  xmlhttp.onreadystatechange = function() {
		if (this.readyState == 4 && this.status == 200) {
		  var response = JSON.parse(this.responseText)
		  document.getElementById("lstDestPort").value = response.lstDestPort;
		}
		else {
		  document.getElementById("lstDestPort").value = "";
		}
	  };
	  
	  xmlhttp.open("GET", url, true);
	  xmlhttp.send();
	}
<%End If%>

<% 'Carie: CRF - Formal Entry Lodgement Enhancement v1.0 - cltcode: FEDEX,  mded: Start at 4, IED-4, IE-4 ,5A-A

%>
	// Consignee
	function searchConsignee() {
	  var xmlhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();
	  var url = "cws_impdecSearchConsignee.asp";
	  var ConsigneeNameTin = document.getElementById("txtTIN").value;
	  
	  url += "?ConsigneeNameTin=" + ConsigneeNameTin;
	  xmlhttp.onreadystatechange = function() {
		if (this.readyState == 4 && this.status == 200) {
		  var response = JSON.parse(this.responseText)
		  document.getElementById("lstConsignee").value = response.lstConsignee;
		  document.getElementById("txtConAddr1").value = response.txtConAddr1;
		  document.getElementById("txtConAddr2").value = response.txtConAddr2;
		  document.getElementById("txtConAddr3").value = response.txtConAddr3;
		  document.getElementById("txtConAddr4").value = response.txtConAddr4;
		}
		//else {
		//  document.getElementById("lstConsignee").value = "";
		//  document.getElementById("txtConAddr1").value = "";
		//  document.getElementById("txtConAddr2").value = "";
		//  document.getElementById("txtConAddr3").value = "";
		//  document.getElementById("txtConAddr4").value = "";
		//}
	  };
	  
	  xmlhttp.open("GET", url, true);
	  xmlhttp.send();
	}
<%End If%>
</script>
<script>
$(document).ready(function(){
    <%If UCASE(Session("CLTCODE")) = "FEDEX" AND (Ucase(Session("mod_cod")) = "8ZN" OR Ucase(Session("mod_cod"))="8ZE") then%>
        $('#lstDestPortName').on('keyup', function(){
            var query = $(this).val();
            
            if(query !== ''){
                $.ajax({
                    url: 'cws_impdecAutocompletePdest.asp',
                    method: 'GET',
                    data: { search: query },
                    success: function(data){
                        $('#results').html(data);
                    }
                });
            } else {
                $('#results').html('');
            }
        });
        
        $(document).on('click', '#results li', function(){
            var cuo_nam = $(this).data('cuo_nam');
            var cuo_cod = $(this).data('cuo_cod');
            
            $('#lstDestPortName').val(cuo_cod + " - " + cuo_nam);
            $('#lstDestPort').val(cuo_cod);
            
            $('#results').html('');
        });
    <% End If %>
	
<% 'Carie: CRF - Formal Entry Lodgement Enhancement v1.0 - cltcode: FEDEX,  mded: Start at 4, IED-4, IE-4 ,5A-A
if UCase(Session("cltcode")) = "FEDEX" and UCase(Session("mod_cod")) <> "IES" then
%>
	// Consignee
	$('#txtTIN').on('keyup', function(){
		var query = $(this).val();
		
		if(query !== ''){
			$.ajax({
				url: 'cws_impdecAutocompleteConsignee.asp',
				method: 'GET',
				data: { search: query },
				success: function(data){
					$('#consignee-results').html(data);
				}
			});
		} else {
			$('#consignee-results').html('');
		}
	});
	
	$(document).on('click', '#consignee-results li', function(){
		var contin = $(this).data('contin');
		var conname = $(this).data('conname');
		var conaddr1 = $(this).data('conaddr1');
		var conaddr2 = $(this).data('conaddr2');
		var conaddr3 = $(this).data('conaddr3');
		var conaddr4 = $(this).data('conaddr4');
		
		$('#txtTIN').val(contin);
		$('#lstConsignee').val(conname);
		$('#txtConAddr1').val(conaddr1);
		$('#txtConAddr2').val(conaddr2);
		$('#txtConAddr3').val(conaddr3);
		$('#txtConAddr4').val(conaddr4);
		
		$('#consignee-results').html('');
	});
	<%End If%>
		
});
</script>
